Doi password SDS (pass SDS, doi pass)
Các b?n vui lòng tham kh?o nh?ng qui t?c don gi?n d? d?i password m?i trên SDS du?i dây:
 
- Password ph?i bao g?m ch? và s?, có d? dài t? 6 d?n 10 ký t?.
 
- Password ph?i có ít nh?t 1 ký t? s?, 2 ký t? s? không du?c n?m c?nh nhau, ví d? password "abc12de" là không h?p l? vì các ch? s? "1" và "2" n?m c?nh nhau
 
- M?t ký t? trong password m?i ch? du?c dùng t?i da 1 l?n, ví d? password "abc3cd" là không h?p l? vì ký t? "c" du?c dùng 2 l?n
 
- Ký t? ? cùng 1 ví tri trong password cu và password m?i không du?c gi?ng nhau, ví d? v?i password cu là "abc1def", password m?i là "acd3efg" là không h?p l? vì ? v? trí s? 1 trong password cu và password m?i d?u là ký t? "a"
 
- Password m?i không du?c trùng v?i 32 password cu tru?c dó.
 
G?i ý d?i password: ví d? password cu là "abc1def" thì có th? d?i password m?i là "bcd2efg"
 
V?y là các b?n th?y d?i password trên SDS cung không quá ph?c t?p ph?i không ? ? Chúc các b?n thành công !

Xu ly A/R bi treo owing, cap nhat docno neu co (docno=0) (treo cong no)
1. can cu chung tu user_ dua qua, minh xem thong tin chu yeu cac field nhu, CUST, TTYPE,ARPAT,DOCNO,ARVAL,AROWNG
2. Nhu truong hop chung tu 27/06/2013, SysAid: #26263
SELECT CUST, TTYPE,ARPAT,DOCNO,ARVAL,AROWNG
FROM ARD	
WHERE ARDDEL='' AND CUST='C01667' AND TTYPE='IV' AND ARPAT='IV' AND
DOCNO=69038558
3. Se thay 1 dong, va cap nhat lai owing= 0 bang cau lenh
UPDATE  ARD  SET AROWNG=0                                          
WHERE ARDDEL='' AND CUST='C01667' AND TTYPE='IV' AND ARPAT='IV' AND
DOCNO=69038558
4. Tuong tu cap nhat owing lai theo yeu cau user_
SELECT CUST, TTYPE,ARPAT,DOCNO,ARVAL,AROWNG 
FROM ARD

DOCNO=69038558

DOCNO=69038558

 A.CQDCTT, A.CQDCTU

 where a.CQLLVL=b.CQLLVL and a.CQHCMB=b.CQHCMB and                 
a.CQHIMB=b.CQHIMB) 

   INSERT INTO CQD(CQLLVL, CQHCMB, CQHIMB, CQDDES, CQDSTD, CQDEND,    
 CQDQTY,CQDSEQ,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU)                                 
 SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD, A.CQDEND,  
 A.CQDQTY, MAX(B.CQDSEQ)+1,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU                
 FROM ldphuc/CQD A, CQD B                                             
 WHERE A.CQLLVL=B.CQLLVL and A.CQHCMB=B.CQHCMB and A.CQHIMB=B.CQHIMB 
 GROUP BY A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD,          
 A.CQDEND, A.CQDQTY,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU

Chi can up file cua user vao 1 file cqd la du 

Phuc su dung cac buoc nhu sau nhe.
1. CHECK DA TON TAI TRONG CQH ?
INSERT INTO CQH (CQLLVL, CQHCMB, CQHIMB,                        
CQHRST,CQHARQ, CQHCTD, CQHCTT, CQHCTU )                        
SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, ITEM,'N','N',CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU   
FROM ldphuc/CQD A, IM B                                         
WHERE A.CQHIMB=B.IMLVY2 AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM CQH C    
WHERE A.CQLLVL=C.CQLLVL AND A.CQHCMB=C.CQHCMB AND B.ITEM=C.CQHIMB)
AND B.IMDEL='' AND B.IMTYPE<>'UL'  
GROUP BY A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, ITEM,'N','N',CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU 

2. UPLOAD VAO CQD
INSERT INTO CQD(CQLLVL, CQHCMB,CQHIMB,CQDSEQ,CQDDES,CQDSTD,CQDEND,
CQDQTY,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU)                                      
SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, B.ITEM, 1 , A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD,        
A.CQDEND, A.CQDQTY,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU                           
FROM ldphuc/CQD A, IM B 
WHERE A.CQHIMB=B.IMLVY2 AND IMDEL='' AND IMTYPE<>'UL'                    
AND NOT EXISTS(SELECT * FROM CQD C WHERE A.CQLLVL=C.CQLLVL AND    
A.CQHCMB=C.CQHCMB AND B.ITEM=C.CQHIMB AND C.CQDSEQ=1)             
GROUP BY A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, B.ITEM, 1 , A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD,      
A.CQDEND, A.CQDQTY,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU

1.	KIEM TRA TINH TON TAI FILE CQD TON TAI TRONG FILE TAM ldphuc/CQD HAY CHUA?
SELECT count(*)                                                            
from cqd a where exists (select * from ldphuc/cqd b                  
where  a.CQLLVL=b.cqllvl and                                        
a.CQHCMB=b.cqhcmb and  a.CQHIMB=b.cqhimb 
and a.CQDSEQ=b.CQDSEQ
and a.cqdstd=b.cqdstd 
and a.cqdend=b.cqdend)  

---------------
update quota

	update cqd a set CQDDES =(select CQDDES  from ldphuc/cqd b     
				   where  a.CQLLVL=b.cqllvl and                   
				   a.CQHCMB=b.cqhcmb and  a.CQHIMB=b.cqhimb       
				   and a.CQDSEQ=b.CQDSEQ)                         
	where exists (select * from ldphuc/cqd b                       
	where  a.CQLLVL=b.cqllvl and                                  
	a.CQHCMB=b.cqhcmb and  a.CQHIMB=b.cqhimb                      
	and a.CQDSEQ=b.CQDSEQ) 	
---------------
2.	NEU CO THI DELETE(neu khong co thi chi can INSERT la duoc) DI VA INSERT THEM CAI MOI
Delete from cqd a where exists (select * from ldphuc/cqd b                  
where  a.CQLLVL=b.cqllvl and                                        
a.CQHCMB=b.cqhcmb and  a.CQHIMB=b.cqhimb 
and a.cqdstd=b.cqdstd and  
a.cqdend=b.cqdend)  
--
INSERT INTO CQD(CQLLVL, CQHCMB, CQHIMB, CQDDES, CQDSTD, CQDEND,     
CQDQTY,CQDSEQ,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU)                                                      
SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD, A.CQDEND,  
A.CQDQTY, MAX(B.CQDSEQ)+1,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU                                           
FROM ldphuc/CQD A, CQD B                                             
WHERE A.CQLLVL=B.CQLLVL and A.CQHCMB=B.CQHCMB and A.CQHIMB=B.CQHIMB 
GROUP BY A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD,          
A.CQDEND, A.CQDQTY,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU
  
  (Chu y neu insert bi duplicate thi remove duplicate ngoai excel voi 3 key field CQLLVL,CQHCMB,CQHIMB.Sau do vo SQL kiem tra
SELECT                                                            
CQLLVL,CQHCMB,CQHIMB ,count(*)  
FROM ldphuc/cqd    GROUP BY                                        
CQLLVL,CQHCMB,CQHIMB                                              
HAVING count(*)>1 
neu co thi ra excel remove duplicate tip)
----------------------------------------- Truong hop con nhieu dong trong CQD chua insert vao duoc. Phai insert vao them trong CQH nhung dong nao trong CQD con lai chua insert vao duoc. co insert vo CQH
INSERT INTO CQH(CQLLVL, CQHCMB, CQHIMB, CQHRST, CQHARQ, CQHCTD,     
CQHCTT, CQHCTU)                                                     
SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQHRST, A.CQHARQ, A.CQHCTD,  
A.CQHCTT, A.CQHCTU                                                  
FROM ldphuc/CQH A                                                    
where not exists (select * from cqh b                               
where a.CQLLVL=b.CQLLVL and a.CQHCMB=b.CQHCMB and a.CQHIMB=b.CQHIMB)

 A.CQHCTT, A.CQHCTU                                                
 FROM ldphuc/CQH A                                                  
 where not exists (select * from cqh b                             
 where a.CQLLVL=b.CQLLVL and a.CQHCMB=b.CQHCMB and                 
a.CQHIMB=b.CQHIMB)

 CQDQTY,CQDSEQ,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU)

 A.CQDQTY, MAX(B.CQDSEQ)+1,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU

WHERE                                      
A.OTMCDE=B.OTMCDE)

Chu oi,
Em xem va tao icon giup chi nhe
-	Icon report tat ca nhung don hang da duoc CS process tren he thong cho PRN A05.
Thong tin tren report bao gom:
-	Customer  code/ customer name/ warehouse.
-	Order number/ Order date/Order Status/Picking slip/Invoice/ item code/item description/Request Qty/ Suppled Qty/B.O Qty/ selling price/ line value.
-	User create OR.
Thanks em.

SELECT A.TTYPE, A.ORDR as Order, A.COHDAT as OrderDate, A.CUST as 
Customer, B.PSN as PickingSlip , B.INVNO as Invoice, C.MANFST AS            
MANIFEST,B.ITEM, B.CODDES as ItemDescription, B.PRNCPL as Princpal, B.WHS as       
Warehouse, CODOUN as RequestedQty, B.CODUNT as SuppliedQty ,
B.CODUBO as BackOrderedQty, 
B.CODVAL as SuppliedValue, D.OTSSTS AS OrderStatus, D.OTSSDS AS StsDescription,
A.COHCTT as OrderCreateTime, A.COHCTD as OrCreationDate,A.COHCTU as UserCreateOR                                                     
FROM ZPTLIBD/COH A, ZPTLIBD/COD B, ZPTLIBD/OTH C, ZPTLIBD/OTS D   
WHERE A.COHDEL='' AND B.CODDEL='' AND C.OTHDEL='' AND D.OTSDEL='' 
AND A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND A.ORDR=B.ORDR 
AND B.TTYPE=C.TTYPE AND B.ORDR=C.ORDR AND B.PSN=C.PSN  AND B.INVNO=C.INVNO      
AND C.OTHSTS = D.OTSSTS  
AND B.PRNCPL='A05' 
AND A.COHDAT BETWEEN 20130701 AND 20130805           
 
select *                                         
from cod                                         
where CODDEL='' and ttype='OR' and ORDR=27922434 

SELECT * FROM OTS A, OTC B, COH C        
WHERE a.OTSSTS=b.OTSSTS AND B.ORDR=C.ORDR

 select count(*)                              
from issd a                                  
 where exists (Select * from ldphuc/temp b    
 where a.PCLLVL  =b.PCLLVL                   
 and a.IVSCMB  =b.IVSCMB                     
 and a.IVSIMB  =b.IVSIMB )                   
 
 -- check duplicate
  select PCLLVL,IVSCMB,IVSIMB,count(*)    
from ldphuc/temp                         
group by PCLLVL,IVSCMB,IVSIMB           
having count(*) >1  

update issd a set SUB  =(select SUB from ldphuc/temp b      
                          where a.PCLLVL  =b.PCLLVL         
                          and a.IVSCMB  =b.IVSCMB           
                          and a.IVSIMB  =b.IVSIMB )
,ISSSDT= (select ISSSDT  from ldphuc/temp b 
                          where a.PCLLVL  =b.PCLLVL           
                          and a.IVSCMB  =b.IVSCMB             
                          and a.IVSIMB  =b.IVSIMB )           
,ISSEDT= (select ISSEDT  from ldphuc/temp b                    
       where a.PCLLVL  =b.PCLLVL

       and a.IVSIMB  =b.IVSIMB )

kiem tra co allocate bi am trong ngay lam viec

Hi,
Phuong chay cac buoc cau lenh ben duoi hang ngay vao dau gio chieu nhe, neu Phuong ban thi Phuc noi chay kiem tra, moi cau lenh chay Phuong copy du lieu de trong file excel nhu file dinh kem, minh kiem tra hien tai.

CAU LECH KIEM TRA TINH TRANG ALLOCATED, SCHEDULED , PICKED BI AM (-)

1. Kiem tra file item master (IM) xem co allocated, scheduled va picked bi - hay khong
SELECT ITEM, IMSOH,IMSOA, IMSSA, IMSPK                  
FROM IM                                                 
WHERE IMDEL='' AND (IMSOA < 0 OR IMSSA < 0 OR IMSPK < 0)

2. Kiem tra file item warehouse (IW) xem co allocated, scheduled va picked bi - hay khong
SELECT ITEM, IWSOH,IWSOA, IWSSA, IWSPK, WHS             
FROM IW                                                 
WHERE IWDEL='' AND (IWSOA < 0 OR IWSSA < 0 OR IWSPK < 0)

3. Kiem tra file LB xem co allocated, picked bi -?, Neu LBSOH < LBSOA hoac LBSOH < LBSPK thi xu ly lien.
SELECT ITEM, LBSOH,LBSOA, LBSPK, LOCN,ISL#,WHS  
FROM LB                                         
WHERE LBDEL='' AND (LBSOA < 0 OR LBSPK < 0)  

4. Kiem tra file IL allocated, picked bi - ?   
SELECT ITEM, ILSOH,ILSOA, ILSPK, LOCN,WHS  
FROM IL                                    
WHERE ILDEL='' AND (ILSOA < 0 OR ILSPK < 0)  

5. Kiem tra file ISL allocated, picked bi - ?
SELECT ITEM, ISLSOH,ISLSOA, ISLSPK, ISL#      
FROM ISL                                      
WHERE ISLDEL='' AND (ISLSOA < 0 OR ISLSPK < 0)

Phuc se xem thong tin do va cap nhat trong truong hop allocate bi am thanh so luong dung check man hinh ESC/3, nhan Shift+F8 cho 5 file IM, LB, IL, IW, ISL
====================================================================================================================
pick am 
SPK<0
Dau hieu la SPK<0, cach chinh nhu sau:

UPDATE IM SET               
  IMSOH  =  IMSOH   -IMSPK  
, IMCMSH =  IMCMSH  -IMSPK  
, IMSPK  =  IMSPK   -IMSPK  
, IMSAL  =  IMSAL   +IMSPK  
, IMCM3M =  IMCM3M  +IMSPK  
, IMSALY =  IMSALY  +IMSPK  
, IMCM3Y =  IMCM3Y  +IMSPK  
WHERE IMSPK<0               

UPDATE IW SET               
  IWSOH  =  IWSOH   -IWSPK  
, IWCMSH =  IWCMSH  -IWSPK  
, IWSPK  =  IWSPK   -IWSPK  
, IWSAL  =  IWSAL   +IWSPK  
, IWCM3M =  IWCM3M  +IWSPK  
, IWSALY =  IWSALY  +IWSPK  
, IWCM3Y =  IWCM3Y  +IWSPK  
WHERE IWSPK<0               

UPDATE IL SET           
 ILSOH = ILSOH -ILSPK   
,ILSPK = ILSPK -ILSPK   
  WHERE ILSPK<0         

UPDATE LB SET           
 LBSOH = LBSOH -LBSPK   
,LBSPK = LBSPK -LBSPK   
  WHERE LBSPK<0         

UPDATE ISL SET           
 ISLSOH = ISLSOH -ISLSPK   
,ISLSPK = ISLSPK -ISLSPK   
  WHERE ISLSPK<0         

Sau do call check va sua them.

select trong SQL ra xem, lay dung dong data co dung so PSN, ORDR, ITEM cua user cap
 SELECT PSDDEL, TTYPE,PSN,ORDR,ITEM,WHS,PSDUNT
 FROM PSD WHERE ttype='PS' and PSN=53062450 
PSDDEL	  TTYPE	PSN			ORDR		ITEM	WHS	PSDUNT	
	Z		PS	53062450	28632247	P040310	WH1	100

Lay ra tu man hinh Shift F9 (hoac shift F8)
Ref# ---  		Quantity    Serial/Lot#     Location     Whs
PS 53062450      100.000  	Z09922          S01-01-1-1   WH1 		

So sánh so Quantity giua man hinh shift f9 (man hinh shift f9, lay cac cot co chu PS o phan REF#) voi so Quantity trong SQL.
Vi user yeu cau cancel so allocate nay, nen ta se tru di.

WHERE ITEM='P040310' AND LOCN='S01-01-1-1'    
AND ISL#='Z09922' AND WHS='WH1'

from       ZSSATCP  where cust<>''

having count(*)>1

 from       ZSSATCP  where cust=''

RE: Khac phuc loi don hang o trang thai P01 OPS250 o order tracking	(anh Thong)
*************** CHU y: neu pick co ra manifest day du va o trang thai FULL BO thi no da hoan thanh

Hi Chu/Phuc,

Tu luc kho Mondial di vao hoat dong, co 1 so don hang/pick bi stuck o trang thai P01, cach kiem tra va fix nhu sau:
Anh Thong OPS250: 

1/. Neu pick NAY la full backorder (PSHUNT = 0) -> can phai confirm pick nay de cac pick da nhat hang/content check hay confirm tao ra hoa don bang lenh: 

CALL PGM(OPS240CA) PARM('01OPS240CA' 'PS' 'pppppppp'), trong do pppppppp la so pick

2/. Neu pick co so luong (PSHUNT>0), kiem tra so luong trong PSD va IA, neu bang nhau thi goi lenh ben duoi tao entry trong workpool:

CALL PGM(RPG681) PARM('TOP' 'www' 'PS' 'pppppppp' '000' '000' '0' '   ' '
' ' ' 'OR' 'oooooooo'), trong do www la ma kho, pppppppp la so pick va oooooooo la so order    

-	Neu so luong PSHUNT = PSDUNT va PSHUNT>0, trong bang IA ko co so pick nay ma chi co order cua so pick nay va so luong cua order trong IA do bang voi so luong PSHUNT ==> luc do ta se update dong order trong IA do thanh dong PS 
update IA set ttype='PS',batch= so_pick
where ttype='OR' and batch = so_order
Sau do ta se 
CALL PGM(RPG681) PARM('TOP' 'www' 'PS' 'pppppppp' '000' '000' '0' '   ' '
' ' ' 'OR' 'oooooooo')

CADD1 as "Customer Address 1", PLCAR as "Area Code", PLCARD as "Area", PLCTE as "Territory Code",

INDCFD as "Invoice Confirmed Date", $9IJAJ as "Net Qty", $9IJAK as "Net Bonus", INDSEL as "Selling Price",

Dear anh Thanh,

Neu lan sau gap truong hop nay, Anh Thanh dua cac buoc nhu dau de lam nhe.

Truy xuat lai ngay hoa don goc
1. Lay mot so Code Khach Hang de tao file_tam
SELECT A.INVNO, A.INHCFD, B.ITEM, A.CUST                  
FROM INH A, IND B WHERE                                   
A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND A.INVNO=B.INVNO AND A.CUST = 'M00972' 
File INH in ldphuc was replaced.
2. down xuong file_ excel sau do dua du lieu cua user vo, upload nguoc lai

3. Tiep tuc link lay goc o file_ INH, IND
SELECT A.*, B.INVNO, B.INHOIN                          
FROM ldphuc/INH A, INH B, IND C                                 
WHERE A.CUST=B.CUST AND A.ITEM=C.ITEM AND A.INHCFD=B.INHCFD AND
INHDEL='' AND INDDEL='' AND B.TTYPE=C.TTYPE AND B.INVNO=C.INVNO
File INHOIN in ldphuc was created. 

4. File_ duoc tao o buoc 3, link ngay tao don hang o file_ COH va chon lay field can thiet 
SELECT A.INVNO, A.INHCFD, A.ITEM, A.CUST, A.INVNO01, A.INHOIN,
B.ORDR, COHDAT FROM ldphuc/INHOIN a, INH b, COH c 
WHERE a.inhoin=b.invno and b.ordr=c.ordr and a.cust=b.cust          
File INH in ldphuc was replaced. 

 ******************LUU Y khi con thieu vai hoa don ko lam duoc thi lam code nay
	SELECT DISTINCT A.*, C.TTYPE,C.INVNO,B.ORDR,D.COHDAT                  
	FROM ldphuc/TEMP A, INH B, IND                                         
	C,COH D WHERE A.CUST=B.CUST AND A.ITEM=C.ITEM AND INHDEL='' AND       
	INDDEL='' AND C.INDCFD BETWEEN 20130101 AND 20131029 AND              
	B.TTYPE=C.TTYPE AND B.INVNO=C.INVNO AND A.WHS=B.WHS AND A.SUB=B.SUB   
	AND A.INDUNT=C.INDUNT AND B.ORDR=D.ORDR AND COHDEL=''                 
	AND B.CUST=D.CUST                                                     
	AND B.ORDR<>0  AND D.COHDAT<=A.INHDAT                                 
	File TEMP1 in ldphuc was replaced.

2/. Chay cau SQL 
SELECT B.TTYPE,B.INVNO AS NEW_IV_NO                               
,B.CUST,B.ITEM,B.SASDTE AS NEW_IV_DATE,VALUE(                     
C.ORDR,0) AS ORG_OR_NO,VALUE(C.SASDAT,0) AS ORG_OR_DATE FROM      
ldphuc/temp a inner join sas b on a.invno=b.invno and b.ttype='IV' 
AND B.PRNCPL IN ('G03','G10','G11','G07') LEFT JOIN SAS C ON      
C.TTYPE='CR' AND B.CUST=C.CUST AND B.ITEM=C.ITEM AND              
B.SASDTE=C.SASDTE

 from ind a,inh b                              
 where a.ttype='IV'                            
 and a.INVNO                                   
 =   72788914

SELECT DISTINCT prncpl      
FROM im WHERE item in (select item from  
ldphuc/temp)

SELECT B.TTYPE,B.INVNO AS NEW_IV_NO                                    
,B.CUST,B.ITEM,B.SASDTE AS NEW_IV_DATE,VALUE(                          
C.ORDR,0) AS ORG_OR_NO,VALUE(C.SASDAT,0) AS ORG_OR_DATE FROM           
ldphuc/temp a inner join sas b on a.invno=b.invno and b.ttype='IV'     
AND B.PRNCPL IN ('G03','G10','G11','G07') LEFT JOIN SAS C ON           
C.TTYPE='CR' AND B.CUST=C.CUST AND B.ITEM=C.ITEM AND                   
B.SASDTE=C.SASDTE

cau lenh SQL

------------ EXISTS
SELECT *
FROM suppliers
WHERE EXISTS (select *
              from orders
              where suppliers.supplier_id = orders.supplier_id);			  
			  
SELECT *
FROM suppliers
WHERE NOT EXISTS (select * from orders Where suppliers.supplier_id = orders.supplier_id);

INSERT INTO suppliers
(supplier_id, supplier_name)
SELECT account_no, name
FROM suppliers
WHERE EXISTS (select * from orders Where suppliers.supplier_id = orders.supplier_id);

UPDATE suppliers
SET supplier_name = (select customers.name
                     from customers
                     where customers.customer_id = suppliers.supplier_id)
WHERE EXISTS (select customers.name
              from customers
              where customers.customer_id = suppliers.supplier_id);
			  
DELETE FROM suppliers
WHERE EXISTS (select *
              from orders
              where suppliers.supplier_id = orders.supplier_id);
			  
			  
			  
update cot 
update CA B set B.CADSPD= (select C.CADSPD
						from   ldphuc/temp C
						WHERE                             
						CADEL='' AND B.CUST NOT LIKE 'CA%' AND B.CUST NOT LIKE 'CC%' 
						and B.CARTE1 =C.CARTE1 and B.CUST=C.CUST and B.CDA = C.CDA  )
where exists (select C.CADSPD
						from  ldphuc/temp C
						WHERE                             
						CADEL='' AND B.CUST NOT LIKE 'CA%' AND B.CUST NOT LIKE 'CC%' 
						and B.CARTE1 =C.CARTE1 and B.CUST=C.CUST and B.CDA = C.CDA )
						
--------------------- GROUP BY Clause
SELECT department, SUM(sales) as "Total sales"
FROM order_details
GROUP BY department;

SELECT department, COUNT(*) as "Number of employees"
FROM employees
WHERE salary > 25000
GROUP BY department;

SELECT department, MIN(salary) as "Lowest salary"
FROM employees
GROUP BY department;

SELECT department, MAX(salary) as "Highest salary"
FROM employees
GROUP BY department;

----------------- HAVING Clause
SQL HAVING Clause - Using the SUM function example ------------

SELECT department, SUM(sales) as "Total sales"
FROM order_details
GROUP BY department
HAVING SUM(sales) > 1000;
					
					
SQL HAVING Clause - Using the COUNT function example ----------

SELECT department, COUNT(*) as "Number of employees"
FROM employees
WHERE salary > 25000
GROUP BY department
HAVING COUNT(*) > 10;

SQL HAVING Clause - Using the MIN function example -------------

SELECT department, MIN(salary) as "Lowest salary"
FROM employees
GROUP BY department
HAVING MIN(salary) = 35000;

SQL HAVING Clause - Using the MAX function  --------------------

SELECT department, MAX(salary) as "Highest salary"
FROM employees
GROUP BY department
HAVING MAX(salary) < 50000;

SELECT A.ITEM,e0104,f0104 FROM IM A,S01 B WHERE A.ITEM=B.ITEM AND
(IMMTDV<>e0104 OR IMMTDC<>f0104)                                 
File IM_VAR in ldphuc was created.                                   

update im a set                                                    
a.immtdv= (select coalesce( b.e0104, a.immtdv ) from ldphuc/im_var b 
          where a.item = b.item)                                     
where exists (select * from ldphuc/im_var c where                    
a.item=c.item)

a.immtdC= (select coalesce( b.f0104, a.immtdC ) from ldphuc/im_var b 
          where a.item = b.item)                                     
where exists (select * from ldphuc/im_var c where                    
a.item=c.item)                                                       
1 rows updated in IM in ZPTLIBD.

(29093999,29108084,29108432,29108657,

SELECT TTYPE, BATCH, BHSEQ, ITEM, IAQA, ISL#, LOCN FROM IA       
where batch =28793696  and ttype='OR'                            


//kiem tra xem cac don hang nay da duoc cancel va finish het chua
SELECT ORDR, INVNO, OTHSTS, C.OTSDES FROM OTH A, OTS c WHERE     
a.othsts = c.otssts AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ldphuc/TEMP B WHERE 
A.TTYPE =B.TTYPE AND A.ORDR=B.BATCH)                             

//dua vao file tam tong sum cua IAQA
SELECT ITEM,WHS,LOCN,SUM(IAQA) SIAQA                                 
FROM IA A                                                            
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ldphuc/TEMP B                             
WHERE A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND A.BATCH=B.BATCH AND A.BHSEQ=B.BHSEQ        
AND ISL#='' )                                                        
GROUP BY ITEM,WHS,LOCN        

   

----Update Cho IW

                          from ldphuc/temp2 b                       
                          where a.item =b.item and a.whs =b.whs)   
where exists (select * from ldphuc/temp2 b                          
where a.item =b.item and a.whs =b.whs)

Kiem tra tai khoan da post len day du cac hoa don chua (Balancing )
Hi Phuc,

Day la cach kiem tra cac tai khoan lien quan den A/R

1. Kiem tra tat ca INH co mat trong GJ va (INHVAL-INHPPD+INHGST) = tong tai khoan 1311x.
-- Kiem tra xem co trung nhau theo Company khong? file JW la chua post, GJ la da post roi
SELECT MJDKEY,count(distinct CO) FROM JW
GROUP BY mjdkey ORDER BY 2 desc 
      
SELECT MJDKEY,count(distinct CO) FROM gj WHERE gjdel='' and mjdate  
between 20131001 and 20131002 GROUP BY mjdkey ORDER BY 2 desc      

1a. Cau lenh kiem tra truoc khi post len JW
SELECT substr(MJDKEY,1,2) as TTYPE, SUBSTR(MJDKEY,3,8) AS         
INVNO,SUM( JWDEBJ- JWCRJ ) VAL FROM JW WHERE GLACCT like '1311%'  
and substr(MJDKEY,1,2) in ('IV','CR') and 
JWDATE between 20131101 and 20131105 
GROUP BY substr(MJDKEY,1,2), SUBSTR(MJDKEY,3,8)
File JW in ldphuc was created.        
--
1b.
SELECT A.TTYPE, A.INVNO, INHCFD,                        
CUST, INHVAL, INHPPD, INHGST,INHCST,SUB,WHS                     
FROM INH A, ldphuc/JW B                                  
WHERE INHDEL='' AND A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND 
A.INVNO=B.INVNO AND A.INHVAL<>0 AND                                                    
B.VAL<>(A.INHVAL-A.INHPPD+A.INHGST)  

--
SELECT substr(MJDKEY,1,2) as TTYPE, SUBSTR(MJDKEY,3,8) AS         
INVNO,SUM( MJDEBJ- MJCRJ ) VAL FROM gj WHERE GLACCT like '1311%'  
and substr(MJDKEY,1,2) in ('IV','CR') and 
MJDATE between 20131101 and 20131104 
GROUP BY substr(MJDKEY,1,2), SUBSTR(MJDKEY,3,8)          
File GJ in ldphuc was replaced.                                    
2. Nhu hoa don nao chua co trong GJ voi tai khoan A/R
SELECT TTYPE, INVNO, INHCFD, CUST, INHVAL, INHPPD, INHGST 
 FROM INH B 
 WHERE B.INHCFD BETWEEN 20131101 AND 20131105 AND 
 NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ldphuc/GJ A 
 WHERE A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND A.INVNO=B.INVNO AND    
 A.VAL=(B.INHVAL-B.INHPPD+B.INHGST)) AND B.INHVAL<>0

SELECT '01','010','001', '52112.'|| PRNCPL,TTYPE||INVNO||'000',  
SUM(INDPPD) FROM IND WHERE TTYPE='IV' AND INVNO=69235740 AND
INDPPD<>0
GROUP BY '01','010','001', '52112.'|| PRNCPL,TTYPE||INVNO||'000' 
--
01  010  001  '52112.' || PRNCPL  CONCAT                SUM ( INDPPD ) 
 01  010  001      52112.A14       IV69235740000         985,029.00 
--

--Trong hop nay bi sai IV nen cap nhat field debit--
file JW
INSERT INTO JW (CO,DIV,BR,GLACCT,MJDKEY,JWDEBJ)

Process for reviewing audit log in AS400
Besides checking ERP exception reports, AS/400 admin needs to 

1.	check daily system status -> wrksyssts
2.	QSYSOPR messages -> dspmsg qsysopr 
3.	problems -> wrkprb
4.	review audit log of the previous day -> DSPAUDJRNE or use ManageEngine EventLog Analyzer 8 / other free open source log analyser 

Nhom AD goi bao cao tinh hinh SDS / AS/400 truoc 10 gio sang moi ngay, tu thu 2 den thu 6.

a.indseq=b.indseq)                                        
where exists (select * from ldphuc/ind c

INSERT INTO CQH(CQLLVL, CQHCMB, CQHIMB, CQHRST, CQHARQ, CQHCTD,   
 CQHCTT, CQHCTU)                                                      
 SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQHRST, A.CQHARQ, A.CQHCTD,   
 A.CQHCTT, A.CQHCTU                                                   
 FROM ldphuc/CQH A                                                     
 where not exists (select * from cqh b                                
 where a.CQLLVL=b.CQLLVL and a.CQHCMB=b.CQHCMB and a.CQHIMB=b.CQHIMB) 
 34982 rows inserted in CQH in ZPTLIBD.                               
 
 INSERT INTO CQD(CQLLVL, CQHCMB, CQHIMB, CQDDES, CQDSTD, CQDEND,          
CQDQTY,CQDSEQ,CQDCTD,CQDCTT,CQDCTU)                                      
SELECT A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD, A.CQDEND,       
A.CQDQTY, MAX(B.CQDSEQ)+1,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU                     
FROM ldphuc/CQD A, CQD B                                                  
WHERE A.CQLLVL=B.CQLLVL and A.CQHCMB=B.CQHCMB and A.CQHIMB=B.CQHIMB      
GROUP BY A.CQLLVL, A.CQHCMB, A.CQHIMB, A.CQDDES, A.CQDSTD,               
A.CQDEND, A.CQDQTY,A.CQDCTD,A.CQDCTT,A.CQDCTU                            
30553 rows inserted in CQD in ZPTLIBD.

B010190      
	select sum(LBSOH),sum(LBSOA),sum(LBSPK) from LB where ITEM='B010190'
	select sum(ILSOH),sum(ILSOA),sum(ILSPK) from IL where ITEM='B010190'
	select sum(ISLSOH),sum(ISLSOA),sum(ISLSPK) from ISL where ITEM='B010190'
	select sum(IMSOH),sum(IMSOA),sum(IMSPK),sum (IMSSA) from IM where ITEM='B010190'
	select sum(IWSOH),sum(IWSOA),sum(IWSPK),sum (IWSSA) from IW where ITEM='B010190'

SELECT ITEM, SUM(ITQTY) ITQTY                    
FROM IT                                          
WHERE ITEM='B010190' AND TTYPE NOT LIKE 'R%'  
GROUP BY ITEM  
 ITEM     WHS ITQTY  
 B010190  WM1  .000 
 B010190  WH1  5.000 
 
 
 IMLTQI - Location Transfer Quantity In  
IMLTQO - Location Transfer Quantity Out      
-----------------------------------------
select item, sum(IMLTQI),sum(IMLTQO)
from IM 
where item='B010190'
GROUP BY ITEM
 ITEM      SUM ( IMLTQI )  SUM ( IMLTQO )    
 B010190   539.000-        539.000-    

 select item,     IMLTQI ,    IMLTQO             
from IM                                         
where item='B010190'                            
 ITEM                          IMLTQI           IMLTQO      
B010190                      539.000-         539.000-     
update IM set IMLTQI=0,IMLTQO=0              
where item='B010190'                         
1 rows updated in IM in ZPTLIBD.             

----------------------------------
select item, WHS,sum(IWLTQI),sum(IWLTQO)
from IW 
where item='B010190'
GROUP BY ITEM,WHS   
ITEM      WHS SUM ( IWLTQI ) SUM ( IWLTQO )      
B010190   WM1  539.000-       539.000-   

select item, WHS,    IWLTQI ,    IWLTQO    
from IW                                    
where item='B010190'                       
and whs='WM1'                              
 ITEM                  WHS          IWLTQI           IWLTQO     
 B010190               WM1         539.000-         539.000-

and whs='WM1'

from ZSCTPCUST b

and   a.SVNAM  = b.SVNAM

and   a.PLCTE  = b.PLCTE

and   a.CMGRP2 = b.CMGRP2

Cap nhat sub-dist va mass create ISSD
Hi Chu/Phuc,

Cac buoc thuc hien de thay doi sub-dist cua 1 khach hang
1.	Cap nhat SUB trong pending order va pending pick slip
2.	Cap nhat SUB trong pending backorder
3.	Cap nhat SUB trong CM
4.	Dung SQL de xoa cac record da duoc MASS CREATE trong ISSD truoc do

CNYD   - Not Yet Due 
CTOT   - Customer Total Owing                              
CCUR   - Customer Current Owing
		   
 so sanh ARS815 va ZAR959 va so voi du lieu chi tiet trong ARD.
 Update CNYD = CNYD of bao cao ZAR959
 Roi lay SUM(owing) of ARD tr? di CNYD s? ra CTOT. 
 N?u owing m?i tháng tru?c ko có gì thì ta update cho CCUR = CTOT

 ARS814,ARS815,
 so sanh ARS815 va ZAR959 theo not yet due va owing 
 
 ARS048 	
shift F12 				   

-------------------------------------------
-	Duong dan: 1-51-1 -> code order -> 5-1 page down
-	Total owing(tong du no toi han)= current owing + 1 month + 2 month + ... + 6 month
-	Not yet Due(no chua toi han)
-	Total owing of customer Book = Total owing + Not yet Due = Tong du no toi han + no chua toi han (cai nay he thong tu dong lam nen ko can xu li)
- 	Dua vao bao cao ZAR959 va chinh lai Total owing, Not yet Due theo bao cao ZAR959
 
ZAR959 - user yeu cau: tttsu Su Thi Thuy Trang 237
chay bao cao ZAR959, roi sua lai cho CNYD,CTOT,CCUR trong file CM bang voi bao cao ZAR959:
update d?a theo báo cáo ZAR959: set theo luat CNYD = Not Yet Due trong bao cao, CCUR = CTOT = Current Due trong bao cao

C.CQHCMB, C.CQHIMB, C.CQDSEQ, C.CQDDES, C.CQDSTD, C.CQDEND,        
C.CQDQTY, C.CQDQIN, C.CQDQRE, C.CQDQAL, C.CQDCOM, D.CUST, D.CNAME, 
D.CADD1, D.CADD2, D.CADD3, D.CMGRP2, D.CMGRP3, D.CMGRP4, E.ITEM,   
E.IMSDES, F.PRNCPL, F.PMNAME, :@TDTE

File INH in ldphuc was replaced.
	
check file INH xem co bi duplicate hay khong
		select CUST,TTYPE, DOCNO ,INSREF,PRNCPL,GROUP,count(*)     
		from ldphuc/inh                                             
		group by CUST,TTYPE, DOCNO ,INSREF,PRNCPL,GROUP            
		having count(*)>1  
		
		Neu co duplicate thi xoa trong file tam ldphuc/inh di nhung line CR co gia tri >0
		delete      from ldphuc/inh          
		where ttype ='CR'                
		and  insval>0                    
		7 rows deleted from INH in ldphuc.   
		
check xem da co trong INVDSA chua	 
		select count(*)                                  
		from INVDSA a                                    
		where exists (Select * from ldphuc/inh b          
		where a.CUST  =b.CUST                            
		and   a.TTYPE =b.TTYPE                           
		and   a.DOCNO =b.DOCNO                           
		and   a.INSREF=b.INSREF                          
		and   a.PRNCPL=b.PRNCPL                          
		and   a.GROUP =b.GROUP )  
		
		delete                                       
	   from            ldphuc/inh b                
	   where exists (Select * from INVDSA a       
	   where a.CUST  =b.CUST                      
	   and   a.TTYPE =b.TTYPE                     
	   and   a.DOCNO =b.DOCNO                     
	   and   a.INSREF=b.INSREF                    
	   and   a.PRNCPL=b.PRNCPL                    
	   and   a.GROUP =b.GROUP )

2. Upload INVDSC - Upload chuong trinh rebate Sanofi lan 3 Ho Phuong Thao -  Service Request # 54428 upload tra thuong sanofi
Format nhieu cot
=> upload theo chuong trinh rebate cua hãng và không theo s? hóa don IV hay CR nào

SELECT * FROM ldphuc/INVDSC  A                     
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM INVDSC B WHERE                
A.CUST=B.CUST AND A.PRNCPL=B.PRNCPL AND                   
A.GROUP=B.GROUP AND A.INCCFD=B.INCCFD AND A.INVNO=B.INVNO AND A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE)

Neu chua co ton tai thi dung lenh insert nhu ben duoi, neu da co thi loai bo ra va bao voi CS

insert into invdsc                                        
SELECT * FROM ldphuc/INVDSC  A                     
WHERE not EXISTS (SELECT * FROM INVDSC B 
WHERE A.CUST=B.CUST AND A.PRNCPL=B.PRNCPL AND                   
A.GROUP=B.GROUP AND A.INCCFD=B.INCCFD AND A.INVNO=B.INVNO AND A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE)

Doi route 
Hi Phuc, 

Duoi day la cac buoc cap nhat route moi Khach Hang cua user gui qua la trong SysAid va file template upload de thuc hien cac buoc nhu ben duoi

CAP NHAT ROUTE MOI
1. Tren CA
update ca a set                                            
a.CARTE1 = (select b.CARTE2 from ldphuc/ca b                
where a.cust=b.cust and a.CARTE1=b.CARTE1 AND A.CDA=B.CDA),
a.CARTE2=(select b.CARTE2 from ldphuc/ca b                  
where a.cust=b.cust and a.CARTE1=b.CARTE1 AND A.CDA =B.CDA)
where exists (select * from ldphuc/ca c                     
where a.cust=c.cust and a.CARTE1=c.CARTE1 AND A.CDA =C.CDA)

2. check on BOT
SELECT CUST, CDA, ITEM, BOTOUN, ORDR, BOTDAT,BOTSTS,              
PSN, INVNO, BOTRTE                                                
FROM BOT A                                                        
WHERE exists (select * from ldphuc/CA C where a.cust=c.cust and    
C.CARTE1=A.BOTRTE AND A.CDA=C.CDA ) AND BOTDEL='' AND BOTSTS<>'R' 
File BOT in ldphuc was created.                                    
--
SELECT A.*, B.CARTE2                                      
FROM ldphuc/BOT A, ldphuc/CA B                              
WHERE A.cust=B.cust and B.CARTE1=A.BOTRTE AND A.CDA=B.CDA
File BOT1 in ldphuc was created.
--
update BOT a set                                           
a.BOTRTE = (select b.CARTE2 from ldphuc/BOT1 b              
where a.cust=b.cust and a.BOTRTE=b.BOTRTE AND A.CDA=B.CDA  
AND A.ORDR=B.ORDR AND A.ITEM=B.ITEM)                       
where exists (select * from ldphuc/BOT1 c                   
where a.cust=C.cust and a.BOTRTE=C.BOTRTE AND A.CDA=C.CDA  
AND A.ORDR=C.ORDR AND A.ITEM=C.ITEM) AND BOTDEL=''

3. Check on Order pending (Wait OR, Credit, Release PS, Picked,... chua ra hoa don)
SELECT distinct B.TTYPE, B.ORDR, B.CDA, OTHSTS,OTHDAT, B.RTECDE, C.CARTE2            
FROM OTH A, COO B, ldphuc/CA C 
WHERE OTHDEL='' AND A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND A.ORDR=B.ORDR 
AND A.CUST=C.CUST AND B.CDA=C.CDA AND RTECDE=CARTE1 AND OTHSTS IN   
('O01','O02','O03','O06','O07','O08','O14',                         
'P01','P02','P06','O15','O20','O21','P09', 'P10','P12','B01','O31') 
File COO in ldphuc was created.
--
UPDATE COO A SET RTECDE=(SELECT CARTE2   
FROM ldphuc/COO B                         
WHERE A.TTYPE=B.TTYPE AND A.ORDR=B.ORDR  
AND A.CDA=B.CDA AND A.RTECDE=B.RTECDE)   
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ldphuc/COO C  
WHERE A.TTYPE=C.TTYPE AND A.ORDR=C.ORDR  
AND A.CDA=C.CDA AND A.RTECDE=C.RTECDE)

                        where a.cust= b.cust and a.cda=b.cda)

                        where a.cust= b.cust and a.cda=b.cda)       
,               CAEXPD =(Select CAEXPD From ldphuc/temp b           
                        where a.cust= b.cust and a.cda=b.cda)       
,               CASLR  =(Select CASLR  From ldphuc/temp b           
                        where a.cust= b.cust and a.cda=b.cda)       
,               CASLED =(Select CASLED From ldphuc/temp b           
                        where a.cust= b.cust and a.cda=b.cda)       
where exists (Select * From ldphuc/temp b                           
where a.cust= b.cust and a.cda=b.cda)

SELECT A.TTYPE, A.ORDERNUMBER, A.ORDERDATE, A.CUSTOMER,           
A.ORDERSTATUS, A.ORDERSOURCE, A.DETAILSTATUS, A.PICKINGSLIP,      
A.INVOICE, A.INVOICESEQ, A.MANIFEST, A.ITEM, A.ITEMDESCRIPTION,   
A.PRINCPAL, A.WAREHOUSE, A.REQUESTEDQTY, A.SUPPLIEDQTY,           
A.BACKORDEREDQTY, A.SUPPLIEDVALUE, A.DELIVERYNAME,                
A.DELIVERYADDRESS1, A.DELIVERYADDRESS2, A.DELIVERYADDRESS3,       
A.DELIVERYINSTRUCTION1, A.DELIVERYINSTRUCTION2,                   
A.DELIVERYINSTRUCTION3, A.URGENTORDERCODE,                        
A.HOSPITALORGINALDOCUMENT, A.DELIVERYDATE,                        
A.DELIVEREDONDATE ,value(-Itqty,0) AS INVOICESUPPLIEDQTY          
, value(B.ISL#, ''), 0 as EXPIRYDATE,                             
value(locn,'') as LOCATION,value(itcrtd,0) as INVOICEDATE         
,value(itcrtt,0) as INVOICETIME FROM ZPTLIBD/zstockup a left join 
ZPTLIBD/it b on INVOICE =batch and INVOICESEQ=bhSEQ AND           
B.TTYPE='IV'

B.COHOTB, SUBSTR(CHAR(COHDAT),5,2),                                
COHSRC,COUNT(DISTINCT A.ORDR),SUM(A.CODOUN ), SUM(A.CODUNT),       
SUM(A.CODVAL)                                                      
 FROM cod a,coh b, cm c WHERE coddel='' and cohdel=''              
and b.cust=c.cust and A.PRNCPL IN ('G03', 'G10') and               
a.ttype=b.ttype and a.ordr=b.ordr and cohdat between 20140101 and  
20141130 GROUP BY A.PRNCPL, C.CMGRP2, C.CMGRP3, C.CMGRP4,          
B.COHOTB, SUBSTR(CHAR(COHDAT),5,2),COHSRC                    

============================
Scorecard – orders taken by
SELECT A.PRNCPL, B.COHOTB, SUBSTR(CHAR(COHDAT),5,2),                
COHSRC,COUNT(DISTINCT A.ORDR),SUM(A.CODOUN ), SUM(A.CODUNT),        
SUM(A.CODVAL) FROM cod a,coh b WHERE coddel='' and cohdel='' and    
a.ttype=b.ttype and a.ordr=b.ordr and cohdat between 20120201 and   
20120229 GROUP BY A.PRNCPL,B.COHOTB, SUBSTR(CHAR(COHDAT),5,2),COHSRC
